- ID: RESE-0805-X-O802-01
- Hex ID: R8O802
- Name: SMD (0805) 8k Ohm Resistor
- Description: SMD (0805) 8k Ohm Resistor

- Short Link: [http://oom.lt/R8O802](http://oom.lt/R8O802)
